 The tradition of fasting and fasting has been going on since ancient times
 sharir or man ko santulit karne ke liye rishi-muniyon ne vrath or upwas ke niyam banaae the
 That is why every fast and fast has its own importance
 kaamada ekadshi ke din vasudev krishna kii upasna karne se sabakaa kalyaan hoga
 Why is the fast of Kamada Ekadashi important? Worship of Vasudev Shri Krishna on this day eliminates all worldly faults and sins
 manyata he ki jo insaan is vrath ko puri vidhi se kar letaa he uske saare paap swayan hi nasht ho jate hai
 Let's know why this Ekadashi of worshiping Kikanha is so important
 
 
 - sharir or man ko santulit karne ke liye vrath or upwas ke niyam banaae gaye hai
 Ekadashi is the most important of all the fasts and fasts
 - maheene main do baar padati he ekadshi, ek shukla paksh main or duusari krishna paksh main
 - Ekadashi fast mainly worships Lord Vishnu, Krishna and their avatars
 - caitra maas main ekadshi upwas kaa vishesh mahatv he
 -kamada Ekadashi keeps both mind and body balanced and also protects against serious diseases
 - paap naash or manokamanaayon keepurti ke liye kaamada ekadshi kaa vishesh mahatv he
 How to worship and worship on Kamada Ekadashi? Every fast and festival is related to a particular goddess or deity
 kaamada ekadshi par vasudev krishna kii upasna kaa vidhaan he
 According to astrologers, by worshiping Shri Krishna on this day, a person can get rid of all his sins
 - is din subah nahaakar pehle surya ko arghya den, phir bhagwaan krishna kii aradhana karen
 - Offer yellow flowers, fruits, panchamrit and Tulsi Dal to Kanha
 - iske baad bhagwaan krishna kaa dhyaan karen or unke mantron kaa jaap karen
 On this day, if you take a completely aquatic diet or fruit, then this fast will give the best results
 - agar keval ek vela rakhen todusri vela main vaishnav bhojan hi grahan karen
 The next day, donate a meal of food or food to a poor person in the morning
 - is din man ko ishwar main lagaaein, krodh naa karen or jhooth naa bolen
 How will the child's wish be fulfilled on Kamada Ekadashi? It is said that by worshiping God with a sincere heart, every problem can be solved
 agar aapaki santan prapti kii kaamana abhi tak adhuri he to kaamada ekadshi kaa vrath karnaa aapke liye vishesh laabhakaari ho saktaa he
 - The husband and wife jointly offer yellow fruits and yellow flowers to Lord Krishna
 - ek saath santan gopal mantra kaa kam se kam 11 maala jaap karen
 - Then pray to have children
 - fal ko pati-patni prasad ke rup main grahan karen
 What to do for financial gain? Even if there is a problem related to money in your life, fasting of Kamada Ekadashi can be very fruitful for you
 - bhagwaan krishna ko pile phulon kii maala arpit karen
 - After this, chant at least 11 garlands of "om Hriman Laxmivasudevaya Namah"
 - phir bhagwaan krishna se aarthik laabh kii prarthana karen

 yahaan hyderabad house main donon pakshon kii pratinidhimandal stareey vaarta ke baad modi ne kaha ki bharat shiksha, swasthya, krishi, kaushal vikaas, mahila shashaktikaran, urja, aadharbhoot sanrachana or loktantric sansthaaon jaise kshetron main afghanistan ke kshamta nirmaan ke liye ek arab dollar kii raashi aavantit karegaa
 The two sides signed three agreements - Extradition Agreement, Cooperation in Civil and Commercial Affairs and mou on Cooperation in the Peaceful Use of the External World
